Shen Bao Medical and Pharmaceutical Special

A Crisp Haircut 204

— Huang Yiqing

Cutting hair short and being done with it, without combing, brushing, curling, or anything else.

When Chinese people get a haircut, they often give the barber extra tips because the barber handles it meticulously, in addition to the stipulated price. This is clearly encouraging the barber to be more and more meticulous, and the more "complicated," the better. In fact, in the absence of awareness and disinfection of equipment, the more meticulous the barber is, the more likely it is to attract bacteria, and the more "complicated" it is, the more it seems to be particularly "complicated" with bacteria.

When foreigners get a haircut in our country, they only need the barber to use the clippers and scissors to cut the hair short, without dusting, combing, or absolutely washing the face or shaving, and even more absolutely without ear-picking, eye-touching, or nose-scraping. After the haircut, they always take their short hair, take a bath and wash it once. After the bath, they comb their hair with a sparse comb or bristle brush, and that's it. Shaving is always done with their own safety razor. Look at how crisp this kind of haircut is! Are the skills of our country's barbers not that simple? Don't they know that? Why don't they dare to teach it?

The reason for this is very common. Eyes, ears, and nose are such precious and delicate organs, how can they be touched, dug, or scraped, and casually handled by barbers! They have never heard of it in their own country. If they are injured by digging or touching, then "a broken ship has many passengers," which is tantamount to opening the door to all kinds of infections, and even more so in their calculations. Also, who would believe that the face cloths, basins, razors, and strops placed in barbershops that don't know what disinfection is are not infected with bacteria? In their own country, if they suffer from a certain barber's neglect and contract some disease, they can immediately report the barber's neglect of duty to the local health authorities. If the government investigates and confirms it, it can immediately revoke his business license. If they contract some infection or get some disease from a haircut in our country, who can they tell?

(Note: Scraping the nose is extremely easy to scratch the nasal mucosa, causing colds, pyogenic bacteria, erysipelas, leprosy, syphilis, otitis media—caused by colds, meningitis—caused by otitis media (rare). The external auditory canal is dug, and if it is slightly injured, it is very easy to get boils, chronic dermatitis, otitis externa, contact impetigo, cellulitis. Earwax also increases with digging; puncturing the eardrum with pyogenic bacteria is also easy to infect the middle ear. Touching the eyes is extremely easy to contract trachoma, pinkeye—acute mucous membrane inflammatory conjunctivitis, gonococcal ophthalmia, etc. When shaving and washing the face, it is easy to get contact impetigo, erysipelas, syphilis (the latter two are rarer) from the razor, and trachoma, pinkeye, gonococcal ophthalmia from the face cloth (rarer; gonococci die as soon as the towel dries). Combing not only easily stimulates seborrheic dermatitis and dandruff, but if a piece of skin is removed, it is also easy to contract scalp purulent inflammation and erysipelas; in children, it is especially easy to contract ringworm, favus—scabies, head lice, and contact impetigo. Using a brush, new wool brushes are prone to anthrax, and dirty brushes are prone to scabies.)

Although, judging from the situation in our country, involving the eyes, ears, and nose during haircuts is troublesome and useless. We can absolutely eliminate this bad habit and not allow barbers to mess around. As for shaving, because not everyone in the country can equip themselves with a safety razor, they still have to rely on barbers to do it. Wooden combs are sometimes still necessary. Therefore, the compromise is to use them as much as possible. On the one hand, we should refer to the business regulations followed by foreign barbershops and the disinfection methods used for clippers and scissors—one barber should have three or four sets of razors and scissors. After use, they should be placed in a formalin sterilizer for two hours, or often immersed in Lysol solution for disinfection and standby use (in fact, the latter method rusts easily, so barbers are not very willing to use it)—, In schools or other freely managed communities, find ways to disinfect at any time—for razors, clippers, and scissors to be used, a bottle of alcohol can be prepared to teach the barber to immerse them in it frequently: face cloths are best prepared by each person, or still shared, but estimate the number of people who get haircuts every day, and prepare a few more, and teach the barber to stipulate that each person uses a clean face cloth, and at night, it must be placed in a steamer or a specially made simple steamer for a quarter of an hour for use the next day; wooden combs should also be disinfected by boiling, and horny combs should be wiped with alcohol every time they are used. If you go to a barber shop in the city alone, it is best to bring some alcohol or high-quality white liquor (shochu), and wipe the razors and scissors before the barber uses them. It is best to bring your own face cloth, or first teach him to wash it with boiling water, or, like foreigners, just be a "pedantic gentleman," only cut your hair, don't shave your face, and don't bother him with all the "add oil and add sauce" and "dragging mud and water" tricks.

Also, recently some people have even died directly from perming their hair. There are many precedents in Beijing and Shanghai. For people who are not related, this is also very crisp. The author said that this is just dying crisply; to put it crisply, in places where there are no skilled perming hands, it is better not to perm!

The Mission of Medical Professional Group Representatives to the National Assembly 205

— Xu Naili

Political tutelage is nearing its end. Soon, 1,200 national representatives will be elected to form a representative assembly to participate in the National Assembly of the Central Government. These individuals will be the recipients of power from the National Government after the completion of political tutelage, hence they are national representatives. Therefore, how significant are the responsibilities of these 1,200 national representatives!

According to Article 2, Clause 2 of the National Assembly Representative Election Law, 380 representatives will be elected by professional groups. Furthermore, according to the quota list for representatives from free professional groups, medical and pharmaceutical professional groups have a quota of eight representatives. The current election regulations inappropriately group physicians and pharmacists as a single free profession. As a result, the actual number of representatives from physicians in the National Assembly will not exceed eight. When the election is announced, the representatives elected by this free professional group will account for slightly more than six per thousand of the total number of representatives. Nevertheless, the mission of this small number of representatives elected by the physician professional group is extremely significant, differing from the representatives elected by other regional and professional elections. Please allow me to elaborate.

Our country has been labeled the "sick man of Asia." The people generally lack a firm understanding of medical and health matters. Some stubbornly cling to their specious views, while others consider hygiene insignificant, entrusting everything to fate. This ingrained habit is weakening the nation. Furthermore, the number of people addicted to tobacco and alcohol is increasing daily. The lack of attention to the health of women and children has led to an alarmingly high excess mortality rate. The average life expectancy is declining steadily. This is not only a tangible decrease in population but also a weakening of the people's physical constitution. Moreover, this has indirect or direct losses to society and the economy. The only entity that suffers the greatest loss from this situation is the nation. This past spring, the National Physician Association, during its Fourth Representative Conference in Hankou, passed a resolution requesting the Central Government to vigorously implement national eugenics, precisely in light of this situation. This is the primary concern for the representatives elected by the physician free professional group in the National Assembly.

Regarding medical defense, in peacetime, the suitability of medicine and pharmaceuticals is entrusted to the entire nation's people. Various public health measures, whether implemented or not, such as epidemic prevention, tuberculosis prevention, leprosy prevention, and even attention to dental health, all have direct or indirect relationships with the nation and its people. Therefore, the determination of medical and health policy objectives and their implementation cannot be said to be unrelated to national defense. In wartime, the relationship between medical defense becomes even more crucial. Frontline treatment, rear area care, epidemic reduction during wartime, and relief for the sick and injured all require meticulous planning. The determination and implementation of these standards and plans require professional insight and immense dedication to service to be effective.

Regarding health education, it is a crucial task at present. We know that the power of education is profound. The weakness of the nation in the past was partly due to the neglect of health education. Therefore, the representatives elected by the physician free professional group in the National Assembly must clearly recognize the importance of health education and resolutely exercise their powers to determine its course.

The countryside is withering, and poverty and disease are increasing daily. The number of those who are bedridden and unable to afford medical care is countless. Even the middle class struggles with the burden of medical expenses. This directly inflicts health and even life misfortunes on individuals, while the nation and society suffer order and economic losses. Therefore, establishing the principle of medical relief is an important issue at present, and the creation of health insurance regulations is indispensable and cannot be delayed. Its implementation and content must benefit the people in every way, which is self-evident. This also deserves attention.

In recent years, during my service with the National Physician Association, the number of medical litigation cases I have seen and heard, whether consulted by the authorities or reported by colleagues, is countless. The Physician Law has not been enacted, and physicians lack protection. Therefore, the Physician Association has drafted a Physician Association Law based on the resolutions of the Fourth Representative Conference this spring, to contribute to the authorities. This is for the benefit of colleagues themselves, and I especially hope that the representatives will promote the early enactment of the Physician Association Law, so that the protection of the medical profession can be solidified soon, which is no small matter concerning the future of medical affairs.

Overview of the Zhenjiang Rural Summer Health Patrol Propaganda Team (Part 2) 206

— Wang Zhangzao

We conduct injections, lectures, and investigations during the day, and costume performances at night. This not only does not interfere with the work of the rural farmers but also helps restore their fatigue from a day's labor. As for the number of people injected in various places, it varies depending on the level of health education in each location. However, the villagers are deeply aware of the harm of prevalent epidemics, and there have been no difficulties in administering vaccinations. During our theatrical performances, the audience is always interested. On average, the number of people injected in each location is more than 500, totaling more than 4,000 people. The number of spectators at each location is also more than 1,000. We have proven from various aspects that farmers need the benefits of health facilities and the urgency of scientific medical care. If someone comes to promote and establish rural health undertakings, the villagers are willing to agree and assist in the process.

(D) Conclusion

The importance of the countryside in China can be found at any time and any place: in terms of population, farmers account for more than 80% of the national population; in terms of land, agricultural land accounts for the majority; in terms of export goods, agricultural products account for the largest number; other aspects, such as national income and raw materials for domestic industries, are also mostly derived from rural areas. Therefore, the countryside has become the foundation of the national economy. If we want the country to be rich and strong, we should first make the foundation of the country (the countryside) sound.

However, the misfortune of the Chinese countryside, since the September 18th Incident, the countryside has suffered from natural and man-made disasters, and it has often been in a difficult situation of bankruptcy. As soon as we arrive in the countryside, we hear cries for help. On the other hand, the calls for rural revitalization in various places are very high, and their rescue methods are multifaceted: economy, society, politics, education, agricultural improvement, etc. But perhaps no one has thought about the issue of rural medical and health.

To trace the root and seek the source: anyone who wants a sound career must have a sound body. Because Chinese farmers do not know the essentials of hygiene, and they usually lose the way of health preservation, so trachoma, scabies, favus, tuberculosis and other diseases in the countryside are constantly invading the farmers. Especially when epidemics are prevalent, it is even more terrible, and at least four kinds of bad phenomena occur:

(1) Villagers get sick, and because praying to gods and worshiping Buddha is ineffective, they spend money.

(2) Villagers are prone to mistakes because they do not seek medical treatment

Page 20

People.

(3) Villagers are prone to expanding areas due to lack of prevention methods, resulting in increased mortality and decreased population.

(4) Villagers cannot cultivate the land because of illness, resulting in reduced productivity.

In summary, our classmates all believe that we are citizens of China, and in this extraordinary period, we should contribute what we have learned to society. Therefore, this summer vacation, we would rather sacrifice the comfort of the individual to plan for the happiness of the greater us. In addition to patrolling and publicizing for twelve days before and after to promote people's attention to summer health; and each person purchased scientific medical equipment and instruments and went to various central townships to organize village clinics to relieve the suffering of the villagers' diseases. At the same time, we also have to ask the national medical community not to care about selfishness and self-interest any more, go to the countryside to universally protect the lives of farmers; consolidate the economic foundation of the country, so as to prepare for a decisive battle for survival with the imperialism that is invading our country. Therefore, we say: the universalization of rural health and the strengthening of the physique of farmers are also a policy to solve the national crisis.

Q&A on Dental Knowledge (42) 207

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 221) Why should mouthwash be used frequently after a tooth extraction?

Answer: Wounds on the skin in various parts of the body can be tightly covered with sterilized gauze to prevent the invasion of microorganisms. However, tooth extraction wounds are open and cannot be completely isolated from the many microorganisms in the mouth. Therefore, mouthwash must be used to reduce the number and activity of microorganisms in the mouth to reduce the chance of the wound being invaded. In the three days after the tooth extraction, it should be rinsed once every hour, and each rinse should last for more than one minute. Teeth with pus should be rinsed diligently.

(Question 222) What else should patients pay attention to after a tooth extraction?

Answer: Do not forcefully suck the wound or lick the wound with your tongue to avoid bleeding. Do not overexert yourself, and keep your mood calm. Stimulants such as tobacco and alcohol should be temporarily prohibited. Choose soft foods, and chew with the teeth on the other side when eating. If the wound is stuffed with gauze, if you do not go to the doctor for examination, do not let it stay there for four or five days to avoid accumulating dirt and hindering the growth of the gums.

(Question 223) When will the gums heal inside after a tooth extraction?

Answer: It takes about two to four weeks, depending on the individual's physical strength, age, etc.

(Question 224) What are the dangers of pulling teeth by people who hold umbrellas on the street or make dentures?

Answer: They have no knowledge of the principles and procedures of anesthesia and disinfection, and they know nothing about the anatomy and histology of the dental part, so there are absurd claims that a certain tooth is a blood tooth, and a certain tooth is connected to the brain. Their pliers, injection needles, etc. have not been properly disinfected, and the tooth extraction wound is infected by them, resulting in various dangerous inflammations, some of which are incurable, and some of the broken tooth roots are left in place, causing the patient to suffer from swelling and pain. To avoid this dangerous behavior, on the one hand, it depends on the authorities to take strong action, and on the other hand, everyone must have a real understanding and not try it out just because of the guarantee of neighbors and friends.

Common Sense on Hygiene for Diseases of the Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eyes 208

— Tang Renjin

(95) The Necessity of Hearing Examination for School Children

Hygiene is a broad field, generally divided into personal hygiene, public hygiene, school hygiene, and factory hygiene. Personal hygiene focuses on an individual's clothing, food, shelter, and daily life, which individuals themselves should adhere to. Public hygiene seeks the happiness of the public and is promoted by the government. School hygiene aims to cultivate young people with strong physiques and is improved by school authorities. Factory hygiene ensures the safety of workers' lives and is designed by the factory. Among school hygiene, physical examination is the most important. For children, special attention should be paid to their hearing examination. Observing the results of numerous statistics, we know that one-quarter of school children lack normal hearing for speech. The presence or absence of hearing impairment has a significant impact on intellectual development. This is because the ear is the primary gateway for input in children's education. Normal hearing is defined as being able to hear whispered speech (low-volume speech) from a distance of 25 meters or more. If whispered speech can only be heard within 8 meters, it can be felt that input for complete education is difficult. School teachers often misunderstand children's hearing difficulties, attributing them to children's laziness, stupidity, or negligence, not knowing that they are the result of hearing difficulties. From a doctor's point of view, school children with hearing difficulties suffer two kinds of losses: (1) they cannot receive education at the same time and in the same way as other children; (2) they often have suppurative otitis media, which may at any time cause labyrinthine diseases or intracranial complications, and some may even be fatal. In the case of chronic suppurative otitis media, the foul smell from the ear discharge often makes the air in the classroom unclean and easily mediates various infectious diseases (such as influenza, tuberculosis, etc.). If we want to prevent the occurrence of such unfortunate events, it is certainly not difficult. The only way is to entrust a specialist to conduct hearing examinations to find them early and carry out appropriate treatment. However, in fact, it is often not easy to do. Because there are often problems with time, cost, and family. So for convenience, it is best for the school doctor to pay special attention to the examination during the physical examination. At the same time, it is also appropriate to refer to the teacher's report on academic performance, because the quality of performance is often closely related to hearing (as mentioned in detail above). Examiners must not neglect this. Speaking of the policy of hearing examination, it can be divided into five:

(1) The hearing of the left and right ears must be examined separately. One side of the external auditory canal can be blocked with the index finger on the same side. Therefore, the ear side with hearing loss can be accurately diagnosed.

(2) The child being examined must not face the examiner, because they can often imagine the unheard speech according to the examiner's lip movements.

(3) The language used during the examination should also be selected. General specialists often use numbers to examine, which is more likely to obtain accurate examination results. The types of numbers are best one, seven, thirty-seven, forty-seven, seventy-seven, etc. In addition, names such as car, rickshaw, tram, train, tap water, milk, coffee, and Yong'an Company can also be used for examination.

(4) The hearing distance obtained from whispered speech must be recorded separately for each language, so that specialists can estimate the type of disease in the future.

(5) The strength of whispered speech must always be the same, otherwise the results obtained may vary. After the five examinations according to the above, if there are children with

If there is hearing loss, the parents of the child should be notified immediately, explaining the relationship with schoolwork and the necessity of treatment. As for the treatment policy, it is determined by a specialist. In general, more than half of the results of treating hearing loss in school children can be completely restored. But what should be done with children whose recovery is incomplete or whose treatment is ineffective? If we want to solve this problem, we can use a suggestion from the famous German professor Hartmann. His suggestion is divided into three types:

(1) High hearing loss The whispered speech hearing distance with relatively good hearing is less than half a meter.

(2) Moderate hearing loss The whispered speech hearing distance with relatively good hearing is half to three meters?

(3) Mild hearing loss The whispered speech hearing distance with relatively good hearing is three to eight meters.

For children with mild or moderate hearing loss, the seat should be near the podium, especially a seat that is easy to face the classmates. Because in the teacher-student question and answer, the lip movements of the classmates can be used to supplement his insufficient hearing. For children with high hearing loss, the ear with relatively good hearing should face the lecture. As for children with the highest degree of hearing loss, a separate class should be set up, called the hearing loss class, and a special teaching method should be adopted.

Medicinal Plants of Domestic Production (Continued) 209

— Zhou Mengbai

8. Scopolia japonica, Maxim.

(Plant) It grows naturally in dark and shady places, a perennial herb. The rhizome is nodular, the stem is up to 30-50 cm high, and the branches are sparse. The leaves are soft, alternate, petiolate, oblong-elliptic, and the apex is acute. In spring, bell-shaped flowers with purple and yellow colors bloom. The capsule is spherical.

Scopolia was originally Hyosoyamus niger, L. produced in our country. I don’t know when it was mistakenly filled with the name of this plant, but due to many years of habit, correcting it would cause misunderstanding, so it remains.

(Cultivation method) Scopolia has always been collected from wild products to fill medicinal streams, but it can also be cultivated. Prepare the land in mid-November, with a ridge width of two feet. First apply compost to the nursery land, and then plant its rhizomes, with a spacing of one foot between each plant. In early spring, apply more fertilizer. In November, dig out its roots, which is the harvesting period, and leave a part as seed roots for replanting. The harvested rhizomes must have their fibrous roots removed, the soil washed away, and dried in the sun.

(Crude drug) Scopolia root Rhizoma Scopoliae, is collected from its dried rhizomes. This product is nodular, irregularly curved, 15 cm long, and 3 cm thick. The surface is wrinkled and grayish-brown. The upper part of the nodules has concave stem marks, the back is short and large, and the roots are branched, leaving traces of its roots. The cross-section is granular and off-white. This product has no odor and a bitter taste.

(Ingredients) The rhizome contains Allealoid. Alkaloid, which is Hyosoyamin C17H23N03, Atroipin (d-l-Hyoscyamiu), Nor-hyoscyamin Cr6H2rO2N, Noratropin, Scopofamin C17H21NO4, etc. According to the analysis of Mr. Yanagisawa in Japan, its content rate is as follows. Total Alkaloid 0.213%, Hyosoyamin 0.108%%Atropin 0.046%, Noratropin 0.037%, Scopolamn 0.004%.

It also contains Scopolin Cr6 Hr8O9 glycoside. Scopolin hydrolyzes with water to produce glucose and Scopoletin (B-Methylaesculitin) CroH8O4.

The stems and leaves also contain Hyosoyamin, Atropin, Scopolamin, Scopolin, etc.

(Medicinal uses) Scopolia root is used exclusively for Scopolia liquid, or as a raw material for the manufacture of atropine sulfate. Scopolia infusion is a spasmolytic and analgesic drug for treating asthma, neuralgia, stomach pain, etc. for internal use. - - Re-use amount 0.01 cm, and Scopolia infusion can be made into plasters, ointments, suppositories, etc. to treat neuralgia, hemorrhoids, etc. for external use.

Calling people rich means they have a lot of blood, and calling people poor means they have little blood. The meaning is the same.

If you don't bleed, you won't stop. Now people's intelligence, people's cruelty, and people's understanding are nothing more than this.

Cold Noodle Stand 211

Breakthrough 212

— Especially

—— Miscellaneous Mountain Travel Notes

Spending the entire day in a teahouse.

This mountain town's teahouse is not worth lingering in, whether in terms of facilities or hospitality. However, we couldn't care less about these things. We sat on long wooden benches, brewed a large pot of clear tea, calmed our minds, and listened to people from different social strata speaking in different ways, allowing the entire mountain town to be reflected in their words.

"The waters of Xishan Gulch burst forth, and the Mentou Dam market has been missed twice!" The speaker was a small merchant-looking man with a worried and bitter face, sitting at a nearby table: "Old Second, think about it, the losses from those two times aren't small, eh!"

I was already quite concerned about the conditions of the road, and this further piqued my interest. I thought to myself: "The flash flood is probably the reason why the car stopped?" Looking at the others, they remained silent and indifferent.

Later, after much inquiry, I learned that a section of the road at Luoshi Weir was submerged by the flood. The surrounding farmlands had all become pools of water.

On the fourth day, we finally got back on the road. When we reached Luoshi Weir, although the major part of the water had receded, there was still nearly two feet of water remaining. The driver smiled—

"It's nothing. We just need to dash through this bit of water." He gestured, his eyes estimating the dimensions of the road surface, "Unlike the previous two days, that was really impossible. The water could have suppressed the cylinder, causing you to lose control."

After crossing that not-so-wide river, we stopped at a station by the riverbank in the evening. At this point, should we continue or stop here? Everyone was discussing. Due to a message brought by the company, we ended up leaving in the hazy moonlight.

Just as we were about to fall asleep, "Squeak," the car came to a sudden, violent stop. The sudden impact awakened us. The driver hurriedly jumped out to repair the damaged parts, asking us to shine our flashlights on his pale face, with sweat beads as large as beans. We couldn't see a single light anywhere, only the chirping of wild insects.

"Damn it, it all broke down in this place!" he complained, borrowing Ah Huang's flashlight and rushing across the field, shining the light into the bushes.

"Oh no! Oh no!" he shouted as he returned, "This place is called Black Tooth Ridge. Packs of wolves often appear here. Going forward six or seven more miles, like the Nine Turns you passed, is also a dangerous place."

We were stunned, unsure of how to deal with the immediate danger.

Holding our breath, we watched him wipe each of the wires, adding some oil to the screws. The clock hands moved from nine-thirty to ten-thirty. Finally, miraculously, he finished repairing the damaged parts.

"Howl, howl," the rough sounds like a whirlwind swept across the field. Six or seven tall wolves surrounded us, trying to jump into the carriage through the windows. We quickly used iron rulers to fight them off, preventing them from getting in. The driver also skillfully operated the engine, turned on the headlights, and sped away!

One of the larger wolves was still closely following, refusing to let go, and even jumped onto the rear bumper.

"Okay, watch this!" Ah Huang said, pulling out the holster. He smirked, "Boom," a flash of fire, a puff of smoke, and with that sound, it fell off the bumper.

The driver said: "The families living nearby, due to carelessness with their doors, often have their babies snatched into the wolves' mouths."

"Should we be grateful for the blessings of fate?" We broke free from the dangerous encirclement.

A Common Tragedy 213

— Yan Ting

Here, where we live, is a narrow and dirty alley. Running from the beginning to the end of the alley is only twenty or thirty steps. Two small rows of houses face each other, packed tightly together, old and dilapidated.

There's a sand-casting workshop right across from us. Inside, a few small, dark lads spend all day in that dim and filthy workshop, busily working while laughing and yelling in a sharp and strange tone...

This laughter and yelling, in the dead of night, sometimes annoys us so much. However, after a certain period of time, they naturally fade away and are replaced by another sound.

We stand silently, using slow eyes to gaze at the greyish window across the way. That sad, low crying and sobbing often makes us feel heartache inside. "Does this sound like a cry from hell? No! It's too weak and pitiful!..." Thinking this, we all become despondent, tears welling up in our eyelids.

Gradually, in that sand-casting workshop, a tall, thin middle-aged man catches our attention. He leaves every morning, without fail, almost certainly, and doesn't return until late at night. Then, the whimpering and cursing sounds are thrown from the dark window frames, passing through the air pressure, reaching our side.

Clearly, the sobs and curses are emitted from two different mouths, but other than this tall, middle-aged man, we see nothing else. A young lad in the sand-casting workshop, when we get to know each other one day, wipes his greasy little mouth smeared with black soot and says:

"It's been three months. Both of them were laid off from the silk mill, and they argue all day long..."

"Who is the man with?" I ask attentively.

"His woman, who has lung disease..." he answers bluntly.

Then, he innocently, using his bare, greasy little arm, tells me, sketching her figure and outline. Gradually, in front of my eyes, the shadow of a short, sickly, pale-faced young woman with sunken cheeks and yellowish eyes flickers in my mind. Slowly, she becomes clearer and more vivid. Finally, her two dark lips are gently trembling, and then she utters in a mysterious tone, worriedly saying:

"What can be done, the machines in the silk reeling room have devoured my lungs!..."

Her yellowish eyes slowly well up with a few tears, and then quietly disappear!

One rainy evening, I am pacing uneasily in the house. A heavy thud attracts me. I hold my breath and listen. I hear a low whimpering sound.

"I can't live this life anymore..." followed by a nauseating dry cough, coughing so laboriously that it almost makes one suspect that large amounts of blood and sobs are being coughed out. "I'm dragging you down, I'm hurting you, so you should let me go back. We can eat mud and grass roots in our hometown, but here we get nothing..."

The other person sighs heavily and walks away with loud steps.

Page 22

This commotion attracts me, shaking me slightly. So, I quicken my pace, push open the door, and run down the stairs, my heart aching.

The alley is quiet, the rain is falling misty. I squint through the dense rain, looking at the sand-casting workshop. The door is ajar, and in a quiet corner, I see a large shadow wriggling, occasionally emitting bitter moans, "It's her, the woman with tuberculosis!" I think quietly.

The next day, the woman with tuberculosis dies in the alley, and the tall middle-aged man is never seen again.

Home 214

— Li Wen

—— Scattered Notes from Within the Profession

Arriving home, I felt that everything had changed. What I first acutely perceived was that the traces of decline had emerged from every corner, irrepressibly, making every facade seem forced and sustained with effort.

Three years is a brief time for those wandering outside; unknowingly drifting outside for three years, returning home, I realized how long that time truly was!

Father has aged greatly, and the signs of old age have clearly crept into his bones. He has become silent, and the dense wrinkles on his forehead also reveal weariness. What makes me most uncomfortable are his eyes, which contain an unreserved joy and sorrow; he watches me like that, without letting go and without interruption; it's as if he has regained a lost treasure but is also worried about losing it again.

Mother, white hair has begun to relentlessly settle on her head! She had a serious illness last year, and her left eye has become clouded as a result. She still hasn't fully recovered her health; however, all this cannot hinder her excessive joy. She personally busies herself, arranging my bedroom, preparing some exquisite dishes that I liked when I was at home; as if forgetting that my return is only for a short stay, or perhaps hoping that I can be more comfortable during this short period.

——I am a stranger to home now!

I sighed uneasily, deeply feeling that I have become a stranger at home.

——Three years!

I increasingly feel that this is a long, and overly long, time.

I begin to hesitate. I never imagined that in the three years that passed so quickly for me, all the changes would have progressed so severely.

"Yun'er, you should rest too. You've been flying around like dust for so long—now, it's rare to come back…"

Mother's voice grows hoarse as she speaks.

I turn my back, my eyes becoming blurry and misty.

I feel uncomfortable—almost wanting to hug my mother and wail, and loudly tell her that I will stay here from now on…

Father seems to understand me, and with his low, disappointed tone, forces a smile and says:

"However, a man, a real man, can't stay at home forever anyway. I say—I say…but in recent years, the situation in Nanyang (Southeast Asia) has been bad, and the Netherlands government intentionally made the Pajak (Note 1) very high…I see—this place isn't a place to stay for long either. Now that you're back, it's just right. I want to take this opportunity to clear things up and find a chance to quit."

I know it's very difficult for Father to say these words. His face is dark and gloomy, and I see that he's getting older.

"Perhaps you don't understand the situation outside—" Father continues, "We Chinese are practically hanging ourselves here! The situation is so bleak, but the Pajak is drawn so high. Yun'er, it's scary to talk about! For example, in Gangkemon (Note 2), a small Aron (Note 3), imagine, how much is the goods worth? It's just small daily sales, and it's still cents of transactions, but, alas! It's scary, but the Pajak is more than five hundred Guilders! (Note 4) How can small businesses survive this! Many have simply abandoned their shops and run back to China with nothing (Note 5), and there are almost hundreds of them on each ship!

"Our place hasn't been approved yet. If things go wrong at that time, it'll be difficult. We have a lot of dead stock (Note 6), and we can't sell it off for a while, it's really hanging ourselves!

"So I say it's good that you want to go back. We Chinese will eventually return to China. Even dying in our own country is more peaceful!—However, I'm old, and clearing things up won't be smooth right away. I think you should stay at home for a few more days. Firstly, to reassure your mother, who has been worrying about you day and night for three years! Secondly, to help me with my shortcomings. When that time comes, we'll go back together!…"

Father's words are like a whip, lashing at my heart, at every nerve fiber. A strange feeling creeps into my senses, suffocating me with an unusual, oppressive discomfort.

"We…we quit and go back?…" I stammer.

Father sighs heavily. "What else can we do? The situation is so bleak, and the Pajak is so heavy—sigh, sigh, Yun'er, they're anti-Chinese, I've heard many people say it, the Dutch are anti-Chinese!…"

Mother brings over the beef broth she made herself.

"This is your favorite! Isn't it? Eat it, I haven't seen you eat anything for three years!…"

As she speaks, Mother's voice grows hoarse again.

Before my eyes, everything seems to be blurring again.—Quit, Pajak, bleak situation, Father is old, Mother is also old, anti-Chinese, anti-Chinese, anti-Chinese…These things are tightly intertwined in my mind, starting slowly and then spinning quickly, I feel dizzy, I hold my head, I fall down—into Mother's arms…

Note 1: Pajak refers to income tax. Dutch.

Note 2: Gangkemon refers to a village. Betawi language.

Note 3: Aron refers to a small business shop. Also Betawi language.

Note 4: Guilder is the name of Dutch currency.

Note 5: "Running away with nothing" means escaping with nothing.

Storytelling 217

Cao Xiaoying's Jade Dragonfly

Central and Western (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening Chapter of Romance of the Western Chamber "Long Story"

Separation and Reunion, Joy and Sorrow, One Cup of Wine. At the Long Pavilion, a feast is held to see off the Autumn Leader. Only because the Madam forced the test, I had no choice but to make a trip to the capital. Only seeing the shadow of farewell grief in the blue clouds beyond the sky. The ground is covered with chrysanthemums, stirring sad thoughts. Thinking of Liang Hao ascending to the clouds in sweet dew. Sooner or later, it will be difficult to defy fate. I steadily climb the fairy laurel in the Moon Palace. I vow not to return without a name on the golden list. Brother. You must cherish yourself in the windy and frosty inn. Don't rush the long journey by saddle. The horse walks slowly. The carriage follows closely. The shadow of the setting sun urges with a whip. Don't think of the beauty of the imperial capital in spring. Return to your hometown with glory and fine clothes. Good things are always hard to come by. Don't hang your bad fate on your chest. River fish and wild geese should be entrusted. Look forward to the gilded report. There are countless words of concern that can't be said. Can't help it. The chaotic dust blows on my face. The most bitter thing in life is separation. I will separate after sending you a thousand miles. Two hearts will accompany each other in dreams tonight.

He Yunfang He Qinfang Double Pearl Ball

Lin Ji (1220) 2:15 PM to 3:00 PM
